Private Estimates of American Cotton

New York, 5th: The average number of New York Cotton Exchange brokers estimated for the current new cotton season is 12,568,000 bales, an increase of 216,000 bales from the last time (September 7th). In addition, Chicago Penny & Company's current estimate is 61.7% of the normal annual production, or 11,491,000 bales, and the amount of ginned cotton is 5,557,000 bales.

Grain: Rice Shipments to He Xia Significantly Increase After the Holiday

(South of Shanghai) Yesterday, there were more than 30 sources, and the market continued to show vigor. Recently, due to the small amount of inventory in stores before the festival, they are now preparing to purchase successively after the holiday. Therefore, the opening market was very active. Later, due to the limited number of arriving ships, the price has been seeing increase. Although the guest banks have not moved, it has no impact. There was no sign of any decline until the close. However, the market prices of various goods varied. The price of each broken indica rice (破粳) rose by about 2 cents, while the price of thin rice was higher by about 1 to 2 cents. Each new tip rice (新尖) was slightly better by a cent. The price of kiln-dried Baige and other types also increased by more than a cent. Yin Yuan (陰元) is still popular, while Bian Yuan (變元) has no market.

(North of Shanghai) Yesterday, there were 31 or 2 sources in He Xia. All kinds of destiations were weak. However, the shipment of broken indica rice continued, and the market price for medium-grade white broken indica rice was close to one foot higher. The medium-grade new indica rice showed a slight tightening trend. The prices of new and old Yangdu customer tips (羊杜客尖), group tips (團尖), water chestnut tips (茭白尖), and other types did not fluctuate much. The kiln type of thin indica rice (薄粳窰種) was close to one foot. Dongxin indica rice (東新粳) increased by another 2 cents.

Inferior Rice Weak and Declining in Price

—High-Quality Rice Sales Decreasing—

Yesterday, the price of inferior rice declined because a large number of rice carts arrived in Shanghai, the inventory was full, and sales were not as brisk as before. Consequently, the various grades of middle and inferior rice generally fell in price. Rice of above-average quality was sought after by merchants from Fujian, Guangdong, and local businesses, maintaining a stable market. However, the provinces of Guangdong are now directly procuring from Hunan and Anhui, and these regions are also planning to transport as much rice as possible to Shanghai. Therefore, the future market conditions for inferior rice are difficult to predict. It is hoped that sales will increase in Fujian, Zhejiang, and locally, and that new markets in Northern China can be developed to sustain the upward trend. Yesterday, Fujian merchants purchased 700 bags of processed rice for transport to Beijing, and over 300 bags of coarse Jing rice from Hunan. Local businesses sold 500 bags of coarse rice to Nanjing, along with a small amount of Hunan coarse rice. Ningbo merchants only purchased 100 bags of late-season processed rice from Jiangxi. Shantou showed slight interest in Hunan coarse rice, with late-season Jiangxi rice selling for 7.45 yuan, and Hunan coarse rice selling for 5.75 to 5.45 yuan. Nanjing processed rice sold for 6.65 to 6.49 yuan, and coarse rice for 5.45 to 5.38 yuan.

Flour Auction Suspended for Margin Call Issues; Today's Auction Depends on Negotiation Results

Yesterday, the flour market exchange was forced to suspend auctions due to margin call issues. With the price of flour falling sharply, there were concerns that both long and short positions were at risk. The exchange is currently gathering flour merchants to discuss ways to maintain stability. Whether the market will open today depends on the outcome of the margin call negotiations before the auction can resume as usual.

Foreign Wheat Active, Si Wheat Falling

Yesterday's wheat market saw a generally quiet opening in the morning for all months. The price of foreign wheat from Chicago fell by about 45 cents, while Canadian wheat fell by a smaller amount. Consequently, market sentiment was generally flat. Distant months were particularly weak due to unfavorable conditions. In the afternoon, the market saw a sharp decline across all months. Foreign wheat sellers were extremely active, offering wheat to factories at a price that fell to 4.35 yuan. However, factories were hesitant to accept due to the stagnation of flour sales. The atmosphere of foreign dumping had filled the market, causing distant months to fall even further. As a result, the current month fell by 5 cents compared to the previous day, November fell by 5 cents, December fell by 7 cents, January fell by 7 cents, February fell by 9 cents, and March fell by 14 cents. The current wheat market is not active, and most factories have no appetite. Only Fuxin is engaging in some trading, mostly in medium and inferior grades at cheap prices. Gao You wheat is selling for 3.75 yuan, Tong wheat for 3.75 yuan, Daqiao wheat for 3.72 yuan, and Lujin wheat for 3.70 yuan, totaling over 4,000 bags.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Prices Plummet

Lyon Raw Silk Declines Another Franc

According to reliable information from the Sin孚 Foreign Firm, the Lyon raw silk market has been weakened by the massive dumping of Japanese silk, making it difficult for Chinese silk prices to hold. White filature A-grade silk (including brands such as Golden Double Deer and Golden Silver Cat) is now only 91 francs per kilogram, a drop of one franc compared to Friday. When converted to Chinese currency, the price is only slightly above 900 yuan per bale.

Export of Yellow Silk Waste to Germany Languishes

Sales of yellow silk waste to Germany have been sluggish for a long time, and exports are dwindling. Yesterday, the German postal ship sailed from Shanghai to Hamburg, carrying only 54 pieces of Jiangbei tail silk and Sichuan scarves from firms such as Fulaide.

Silk Sales to Europe and America Lacking Vigor

Recently, labor strikes have spread among silk weaving factories in New York and other places, leading to a decrease in raw silk consumption. General hoarders are actively competing to sell their stocks. The dumping of Japanese silk in Lyon and England continues unabated, causing silk prices to plummet. Telegraphic silk prices are also falling. New York B-grade filature is priced at only 620.30 yuan, making it even more difficult for factories to sell. The market is quiet. Yesterday, only Dafeng and others imported 30 bales of yellow and white filature, with prices continuing to decline.

Sugar Market: About 200 Bags of Green Sugar Traded

Yesterday, the sugar market saw a slight decrease in customs gold and a slight increase in Dutch exchange rates, leading to a trend towards stabilization. The Association's clearing price for 24-grade sand white ordinary goods was 21.58 yuan, with some transactions. 20-grade medium sand was quoted at 20.9 yuan, 18-grade at 20.7 yuan, high-grade Dutch red sugar MKGB was quoted at 16.9 yuan, and NT mark at 10.6 yuan, but no transactions occurred. China Guohua Zhenji No. 1 cotton white was quoted at 20.6 yuan, and Taikoo B mark at 21.65 yuan. Chaozhou firms quoted village green sugar at 16 yuan, followed by 15.8 to 15.3 yuan, totaling over 100 bags. Jianbang firms offered 100 bags of oily package green sugar at 14.7 yuan. The inventory of high-grade Chaozhou green sugar is not large, and land prices are relatively firm, leading to a tightening of prices.

Dried and Fresh Produce: Some Quanzhou Large Longans Sold

The first batch of Quanzhou large blister longans, which arrived recently via Jianbang, was displayed yesterday. Top-grade large-sized goods are priced at around 80 yuan, with subsequent grades varying by 23 to 45 yuan. However, the lower grades face competition from other routes, making it difficult to develop and sell well. It is expected that sales will continue today.

Metals: Union Iron Oversupply

The Union Iron has recently been overstocked with new arrivals, but sales are limited, leading to an oversupply. Standards are gradually being relaxed, and the current market price is only 30 yuan, a decrease of 5 cents compared to before. It is rumored that large-scale transactions can be made for about 1 yuan cheaper.

Oil Market: Asphalt Trend Weakening Daily

The asphalt market has been unusually sluggish since autumn, with the largest stockpiles in Hankou. For example, the total amount of Macheng oil is over 10,000 pieces, and the total amount of Chongjing, Pingjing, Zhijiang, and Jinshi oil is over 30,000 pieces. However, sales are only sporadic. Soap factories are not interested in asphalt because beef tallow and coconut oil are cheaper. The amount used by candle makers is extremely limited. As a result, many merchants from Jing, Xuan, Zhi, Jin, and Ma are transporting oil to Hankou for sale, leading to a larger stockpile in Hankou than in spring and summer. In previous years, the old oil would gradually sell out as new oil was about to be produced in autumn, but now the stockpile in Hankou is larger, making it inevitable that the market will fall sharply. The repeated price drops in the past month are due to this. Recently, the Mid-Autumn Festival has been busy with settling accounts, further reducing transactions. Although the stockpiles in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are relatively thin, it is unlikely that they will be sold out before the new production. Therefore, Hankou's hope for sales to Jiangsu and Zhejiang is fading. It is rumored that Chongjing oil in Hankou is only selling for 20 yuan, and Macheng oil may not be able to hold at 19 yuan. The trend of prices plummeting is obvious. However, there may be some candle sales after the Mid-Autumn Festival, which may help to stabilize the market. Local merchants already have limited stockpiles, but due to sluggish sales, they have to further reduce prices to stimulate interest from candle makers. The listed price for Chongjing oil is 24.5 yuan per dan, Pingjing oil is 24 to 23.5 yuan, and Macheng oil is 22.5 yuan per dan. However, these prices are nominal, and the actual prices are falling in secret. The disparity between listed and actual prices is a common practice due to the poor market conditions.

Light-skinned Peanut Oil Plunges One Yuan

After the price drops in Jia Cang, Boer, and Jiaozhou peanut oil, light-skinned peanut oil has not been traded for over a month because buyers are not interested and the stockpiles are small. The market is stagnant for both peanut and soybean oil. Therefore, sellers are selling 300 pieces of light-skinned peanut oil at a low price to boost market confidence. The price is 13.1 yuan, a sharp drop of over one yuan compared to the previous closing price.

Fashion Special Issue, No. 5

Fashion and Its Economic Impact: Peculiar Interests, Wild Decorations

— Xu Yunshou

Fashionable clothing and luxurious decorations have become almost essential for a modern woman. Styles, colors, and patterns change rapidly and constantly, making them unpredictable. People do not know their origins, nor where they are going. Women who love fashion only know what is popular and what to wear, without knowing why. However, society is becoming increasingly extravagant and Westernized due to the changes in fashion, which has sparked countless praises and criticisms. Therefore, discussing this issue is of interest today.

On the surface, it seems like a simple problem, but a detailed study reveals endless difficulties. I have not researched this topic, but I will discuss it based on the views of others for clarity, I will divide the discussion into three parts:

(1) What is fashion?

(2) How is fashion created?

(3) The economic impact of fashion

We can say that fashion is a habitual need for change. It is dynamic, never fixed, and unimportant. It makes people unaware of the changes in the most trivial patterns and shapes. The French Voltaire once said:

It is a beautiful woman without constancy, without habit, and without peace.

Peculiar are its interests, wild are its decorations.

It seems to have fled, but it still returns slowly, always living forever.

Its father is the indecisive, and its name is fashion.

We must admit that humans are slaves to fashion. Fashion follows human whims and is the most unreasonable and chaotic medium for new patterns.

Hard Collars on Qipao

In fact, fashion is as old as the world, and also eternally new if we look back. However, the return is only a modified appearance. To verify this, we only need to compare the Manchu qipao with modern women's clothing to understand. Even the high and hard collars currently in fashion are similar to the ingot collars of twenty years ago. Despite this, women's fashion is extremely complex and elusive. It does not obey rules, nor is it subject to laws. We can summarize fashion in the words of Virgil:

Happy is the one who knows the causes of things.

In fact, fashion has its own principles, but the truth is not recognized.

Bare Arms, Exposed Legs, and High Heels

So how is fashion created?

The history of fashion throughout the ages often points out that trivial reasons, changes, and accidental events often involve a fashion that spreads throughout the world, leaving special and permanent traces in history. Sometimes the appearance of fashion is often caused by the eccentricity of a princess, the entertainment of a queen, or by a drama or political change, as in the following examples:

King Louis XI of France's daughter created long clothes that dragged on the feet because her feet were too big.

The beautiful Ferronnicre had a burn scar in the middle of her forehead, so she wore a jewel attached to a thin thread to cover the scar.

Queen Anne of Austria, whose arms were extremely white and full, created the fashion of bare-armed, sleeveless clothes.

Madame de Pampadour, with her graceful waist, created high-heeled slippers without backs.

In China, the change of dynasties brought about changes in clothing. Not to mention the recent success of the revolution, which led to the popularity of the Zhongshan suit. With the names of curvy beauty and others, close-fitting, leg-revealing clothes came into being. At the same time, women wore high-heeled leather shoes and permed their hair.

Autumn Style New Crepe Gui and Pleated Qipao

— Ms. Xuanxiang

I have never relied entirely on tailors for my clothing, nor have I wished to imitate the fashionable clothing of the moment, because women's clothing in Shanghai was often first created by prostitutes, and the ladies and misses would imitate them.

Autumn clothes are the most difficult, because there will be wind and rain, especially at night, when it is relatively cool. Therefore, it is difficult to make clothes that are both beautiful and suitable for the weather.

In the autumn when it is cool but not cold, it seems too early to carry an autumn coat, and it also does not seem very beautiful to wear a woolen half-sleeve.

Now I have made a set of clothes for myself, one called "Gui" (i.e., short cape) and the other is an ordinary qipao, with slight changes. The qipao is made of silk crepe, with very long sleeves, but the cuffs are all made of elastic bands so that they can be hung under the shoulders (like the sleeves of this year's popular women's suits). Because the slits in the dress are very long, it is too cool and not elegant. So, I chose plain chiffon of a similar color to the silk crepe and intricately pleated it into the dress's slits, making the hem of the dress particularly wide, so that it is starry and stylish when walking.

The "Gui" is made of double-layered satin, and it is also unlined. The double-layer is the same on the front and back, one side is red and the other side is black. Either side can be used as the front or back. A three-and-a-half-inch long ribbon is sewn on the collar, which can be wrapped around the neck and used as a scarf, hanging on the back or chest, there is no problem. If the weather is a little warmer, it can be taken off and placed on the arm, which is not annoying. If the weather is a little colder, or at night, it can be worn, which is very beautiful. Since I made it and wore it, many girlfriends and sisters have imitated it. I think it is not vulgar at all, and the style is very dignified and noble, without any frivolity, and it is so beautiful.

。

Pleated Pants and Military Uniform Coat

However, modern Europe and America are slightly different. Almost all fashion is created and packaged by a few large sewing shops. There are also many fashion companies in Shanghai now, most of which still copy European and American samples. These stores hire specialized talents to come up with designs, and then have model women wear them to promote them to the public, like the Shanghai Fashion Conference; or they promote them through advertisements, magazines, theaters, movies, and extravagant banquets. The world-famous fashion magazine Vogue can also be bought in Shanghai. It previews the materials, colors, and strange styles of each season's fashion.

At this point, we will have the following question again: Where do these people who specialize in creating fashion get their inspiration? In fact, there are many sources that influence their imagination. First of all, it is the current facts, special events, wars, etc., that can form a certain fashion or a certain fashion's incarnation. Therefore, during the Louis-Philippe era, all the fashionable young men in Paris wanted to wear pleated pants, like African hunters. Even the Westernization of men's clothing in China in recent years has been influenced by Europe and America to some extent. Some fashions are also inspired by literature; for example, wearing Atapa collars and Marie-stuart brimless hats. Romanticism has expressed special characteristics, that is, restoring national customs and medieval styles. For example, in gold and silver filigree, jewelry has become Gothic, with thick iron hand rings, guards wearing towering moth hair hats, helmets, coats of arms, shields, medals, and the entire feudal manufacturing bureau, all made of gold, silver, carving, and enamel. Recently, the newspaper also reported that Cubists were wearing strangely shaped hats in Rome. And in China, since last winter, the style of women's coats has been the same as that of military officers' coats, with many yellow and white copper buttons sewn on the front and back. At least, like the beautiful clothes of Hifer in the film The Merry Widow, I think it is also influenced by the two wars of [September 18th] [January 28th], and women also have the imagination of joining the army. (To be continued)

The Elimination of Cotton Clothing

— A Thread

Ten years ago, women all wore short clothes, and in early winter, they had to wear cotton-padded clothes. The more elaborate ones were sewn into various patterns with thread. The five auspicious clothes given by Suzhou when betrothing, cotton-padded, lined, unlined gauze, cotton-padded clothes were indispensable. Since the evolution of the qipao, cotton-padded clothes have gradually been eliminated. Because cotton-padded clothes are always a little bloated, no matter how little they are lined. Instead, they are replaced by flannel and camel hair.

Flannel is naturally the most fitting. If the weather is cool but not cold, or if it is suddenly cold or suddenly hot, single-layered clothes are too shabby, and camel hair is too warm, so flannel is the most suitable. In deep winter, leather is too heavy, so camel hair must be used. From an economic point of view, these two are also the most cost-effective.

There are also lined clothes, which are cheaper than flannel, and you can line faded or old clothes, and their effect is comparable to flannel.

In this way, cotton-padded clothes have to retreat. However, in evening makeup, in the boudoir, taking off the long clothes and putting on a delicate short cotton-padded jacket or a thin cotton-padded half-sleeve is very poetic. Bai Juyi's poem: [Gui cloth is as white as snow, Wu cotton is as soft as clouds, the cloth is heavy and the cotton is thick, and the fur has residual warmth.] It can be seen that cotton-padded clothes are much better than leather clothes. Therefore, I think that cotton-padded clothes are not suitable for external wear, but suitable for internal wear, and should not be completely eliminated.

Color Matching Method for Modern Women's Clothing

— Yixiang

(Continued)

White (Primary Color)

White is the purest of all colors, simple and dignified, clean and beautiful, and free from worldly dust. Because it is the highest grade in color, it is also the ancestor of colors. Therefore, European and American ladies use it for their clothes in summer and autumn, taking its cleanliness and superiority, and not staining the dust. Moreover, the accompanying color should be bright and beautiful, because cleanliness with beauty is like a lotus emerging from the water, which is more beautiful. The suitable accompanying colors are listed below:

(Suitable Accompanying Colors) Blue, Rose Red, Han Yellow, Black-Blue

Black (Primary Color)

Black is the most沉of all colors, its容is静穆, its meaning is深濃, occupying the most important position in color. Therefore, European and American ladies like to make it into clothes, because it is elegant and appropriate, and has a generous attitude. However, since the正色is沉, its佐色must be凈, in order to match the position of guest and host, the more brilliant it looks.

(Suitable Accompanying Colors) Red, Blue, White, Gray, Blue-Violet

Dark Gray (Belongs to Black)

Pattern of double-layered winter coat fabric woven from Genuine Camel Hair by Zhanghua

(Suitable Accompanying Colors) Blue, Rose Red, Blue

Gray is also one of the mature colors, dignified and elegant, so people often like to use it. The color matching is as follows:

(Suitable Accompanying Colors) Blue-Violet, Rose Red, Light Blue, Light Purple

Home Daily Update Association and Clothing Standards

— Yangfen

Three years ago, in order to improve the clothing problem, the members of the Home Daily Update Association held a meeting at Mr. Shi Liangcai's residence to discuss. The members who attended the meeting:

24 male members, 40 female members, 15 male students, 21 female students. Among the 24 male members, one was over 60 years old, three were over 50 years old, seven were over 40 years old, five were over 30 years old, and eight were over 20 years old. Among the 40 female members, two were over 50 years old, five were over 40 years old, eleven were over 30 years old, and twenty-two were over 20 years old. The 36 male and female students were mostly between 15 and 20 years old. There were also some who were under 15 years old, I don't remember clearly. Most of the discussions were about four types: one was ordinary clothing, the second was Western clothing, the third was women's clothing, and the fourth was children's clothing. The standards of discussion were divided into four categories:

One quality material, domestic, economical.

Two forms, beautiful, brave.

Three colors, simple, elegant.

Four styles, flexible, applicable.

Among these many members of different ages, genders, thoughts, and concepts, these four standards were actually agreed upon, and everyone had no objection, which is really a rare thing. At that time, everyone also took a photo, because everyone was wearing cloth clothes, some people called it the cloth clothes conference. The clothing that each family created was exhibited, and some people interpreted it as a clothing exhibition. Everyone believed that a new era was opened in the family. At that time, the products of Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory were actually outstanding, and won a lot of praise. I accidentally saw this record in my diary, and then I will explain the four standards:

In terms of one material, domestic fabrics can be said to have everything. Silk and satin should be pushed to Meiya, wool should be counted as Zhanghua, and cloth should be pushed to Hongxin, all of which are cheap and in line with economic principles.

In terms of two forms, beauty seems to have no standard, but the first is to avoid vulgarity, the second is to avoid anger, and the third is to avoid evil. The main goal is to be magnificent and healthy, and the lines can be called brave. I remember that Hongxin and Meiya spent a lot of research effort on this point.

In terms of three colors, the main goal is to be simple, plain, and elegant, and not to be extravagant, flamboyant, or charming. Once this goal is identified, then silk and satin are good, wool is good, and cloth is good. Hongxiang Company has a lot of old experience in this kind of color matching.

In terms of four styles, wool should be used for warmth, silk and satin should be used for lightness, and national cloth should be used for dignity and generosity. And the overall goal is to be flexible and suitable. Everyone knows that Hongxiang Company has put a lot of effort into this.

After this discussion, family clothing has been reformed a lot, and the easiest to see is:

One is that domestic goods have been adopted, and Meiya, Zhanghua, and Hongxin have done a lot of business.

Two, there are no more people wearing妖艶clothing.

Three children's clothing is all雄糾糾氣昂昂. The little old men with wide robes and large sleeves have actually disappeared from each family.

Four, each family's clothing has certain standards, and the cost of clothing for one year has been simplified, and the family economy has benefited greatly.

Now the small members of the Home Daily Update Association have grown up. Do you still remember the day of the discussion; were your little hands still raised very high?

Free Talk

What Separates Humans from Beasts

— Zhi Li

The representatives of the Anti-War Association have already left Shanghai one after another. A certain English newspaper recently published a cartoon: a ship going out and a ship coming in. The ship going out was carrying several representatives of the Anti-War Association! People, while the ship coming in was loaded with lions, elephants, tigers, leopards - beasts.

Truly gratifying to the people's hearts. Fabricating something out of nothing, causing anxiety, what Marquis Marais and others have exited, let them go to [the Pacific Ocean] or [the bottom of the sea] to hold an [anti-war conference]! And this time, the German Hagenbeck Circus has arrived in Shanghai, world-renowned!

Shanghai is going to be very lively, and Shanghainese are going to be very happy, look, look!

War, why should we oppose it? Needless to say, the Twenty-Four Histories are a book of mutual slaughter. Even in the last ten years, what day have we not seen war? Being used to it, we have long been accustomed to it. As for saying it's scary, as long as the bombs don't fall on our heads, what's so scary about it? Who has ever felt scared watching Luo Tong and Pan Yang fight a great battle on stage? Moreover, that's so interesting! Ruskin didn't say, [War is the largest and most valuable kind of sport (Game) conducted by mankind.]? War is originally a Game, it's a Sport, that's such a happy thing! Who doesn't want to see the Spanish bullfight, who doesn't want to see the ancient Roman Gladiator? The Far East Games, the National and Provincial Games are already so lively, let alone the world war [spectacle]? Besides, when the First World War was happening, didn't we calmly sit on the sidelines, and didn't we become one of the victorious nations afterward?

War, why should we oppose it? Besides, the Hagenbeck Circus is not welcomed by the whole world? Inside are all lions, elephants, tigers, leopards, savage beasts. Are humans more savage than beasts? Is mankind's large-scale competition not as good as beasts' large-scale competition?

Go, you Marquis Marais and your group, go elsewhere!

Welcome, German Hagenbeck Circus!

Shanghai is going to be very lively, and Shanghainese are going to be very happy, look, look!

Mencius said, "[What separates humans from beasts is but a trifle]?"

Someone replied, "[It lies in one going out and one coming in]."

On Liu Kezhuang's Poetry

— He Ru

During the Southern Song Dynasty, there was the so-called Jianghu Poetry School. This was because a bookstore owner, Chen Qi, compiled and printed the Jianghu Collection, hence the name. Although this school of poets, like the Four Spirits School of poets at the same time, studied the late Tang Dynasty in poetry, they did not pay much attention to the refinement of words and sentences. They liked to write satirical poems and use recent events as poetic material. Moreover, some people used poetry to seek patronage and engage in self-promotion, severely exploiting others, such as Song Qianfu visiting Jia Sidao and obtaining 200,000 strings of paper money to build luxurious houses. These poets were truly worthy of being called "[traveling the Jianghu]"!

The famous Jianghu poets include Liu Kezhuang, Yue Lefa, Dai Fuguo, Ye Shaoweng, Liu Guo, Jiang Kui, and Fang Yue, among whom Liu Kezhuang's poetry is the most famous. Liu Kezhuang wrote many poems in his life, with the number between Lu You and Yang Wanli. He has his own poem to prove it:

Ode at Eighty (One of Ten Poems Recorded)

Cheng Weng only has four thousand poems, while Fang Weng nearly fills ten thousand. The old man has remnant brocade in his chest, asking Heaven to grant him Fang Weng's years. Originally, he greatly admired Yang Chengzhai and Lu Fangweng, and this is also proven by his poems:

Inscription on Fang Weng's Portrait

The Three Hundred Poems have been silent for a long time, and the nine thousand poems are all new.

Like the First Ancestor in Zen Buddhism, the only one since crossing the Yangtze River.

Inscription on Chengzhai's Portrait

A man beside Ouyang Gong's house, poetry outside the Lu Donglai school.

The world unanimously praises him as unparalleled, and a branch emerges from Jiangxi.

Even in his old age, he did not forget to catch up with Lu and Yang's status. His "Rising from Illness" poem says:

Since the changed customs, there has been no poetry in the world. Initially learning Xikun, I was ashamed of being pretentious. In old age, I am merely known as a minor figure, having once known the great masters. In a hundred years, I unknowingly have white hair at the temples. Who can sever countless whiskers? How many days will Chengzhai and Fangweng die? I will whip myself ten thousand times to follow them. His poems have two characteristics: one is that he likes to write six-character quatrains, and the other is that he likes to use stories from the current dynasty. Poets have always believed that using ancient events is better, but he prefers to use recent events that are familiar to everyone at the time. For example, "[Often mocking Jie Fu for implementing new laws, often hating Ou Gong for not reading books]." "[U Sou invited me to enter Zhen Shuai, but Guaiya would not admire a light carriage]." "[Kangjie's Book of Changes was passed down to hermits, and Lianxi learned it from eminent monks]." "[Villagers only know the beauty of celery soup, how can Prime Minister know the sweetness of eating bamboo shoots!] (Self-note: Fu Zheng Gong's affair)." These kinds of sentences can all be used as examples. He once had a line in a poem that said:

Worrying about the times is originally a poet's job,

Don't blame the many emotions in the poems.

This seems to be one of the reasons why he likes to use recent events in his poetry. However, he has endured criticisms such as "[poor quality of language, shallow and exposed meaning]" or "[glib and frivolous, the last of the Jianghu]."

Records of Ancient Matters

— Xiao Xue

If 1933 is said to be a year of national debt, then cool autumn September is also worth a "[month of ancient object revival]". Ancient objects, at any time are [striving to climb up] from the ashes (respectfully using Dr. Hu Shi's poem), why specifically add the word [revival] to this month? The original reason is that reviving the past seems to have formed a movement, and in recent months, even the air has a bit of an ancient flavor.

If you don't believe me, why not read the [Records of Ancient Matters] in cool autumn September:

(1) It says... Build a Confucius Temple, create a Classics School (Singapore, Reuters telegram).

(2) It says... Limit the use of brushes, boycott foreign stationery (Guangzhou, Reuters telegram).

(3) It says... Ancient tombs are discovered one after another (Nanchang, Shandong special telegram).

(4) It says... Golden marriage certificate, special release (Tianjin, Central News Agency telegram).

[How glorious and holy], a month's achievements are like this. If we continue to work hard in this way, [Han dynasty clothing] will not [become an ancient hill], and our [great nation] will truly have hope of revival. When I'm free and have nothing to do, I always feel happy thinking about this. It's not a fantasy. I think that the people at that time must have been wearing flowery clothes from the stage, swaggering on the official roads, bowing to people, and shouting loudly, "[Greetings, sir]". And when there was a love affair, it must have been that the hero dragged a shiny sword, strode onto the [Mandarin Duck Tower], and had a few more rounds of [blood splattering], so that the X newspaper reporter could write more vividly, erotically, and sensually.

What about the foreign devils? At that time, they wouldn't be as [rampant] as they are now. These Yi and Di countries would definitely be shocked by the [Han Kingdom's prosperity], and would come to pay tribute every year to restore the past glory. Thinking of them crawling on their knees from the Meridian Gate all the way to the Golden Dragon Hall, prostrating and shouting "Long live!" without daring to look up, and even recalling their oppression of China now, their ugliness, it really makes me feel elated. Although I also worry that there will be another Jin Wuzhu or An Lushan at that time.

Judging from historical facts, reviving the past is ultimately good. China has [nothing else to say] besides reviving the past. However, when I think of the [golden marriage certificates] of the empresses of the past dynasties inevitably being bought by [Yi and Di], and even though it is specified to use brushes, it is still unavoidable to advocate using fountain pens to [write English], to the extent that although the [holy temple] has received money, it has not yet been built, and the [ancient corpse turns to ashes as soon as it sees the wind], I can't help but [change color] a little. Alas!崇崇 the present is certainly not possible, and reviving the past is also somewhat vague. After writing the [Records of Ancient Matters], I can only put myself on the [shaking] shelf, [pursue] what?

Roar, China!

— Dong Meikan

The black curtain of night covers the earth, only a few stars twinkle in the darkness, holding lanterns and emitting the light of excitement, I walk in the light of the lanterns, it's hard to say it's early autumn, but the night is quite cold, wearing thin clothes, I feel a slight chill, I walk silently with a belly full of enthusiasm, walking towards the theater, on the streets where the noisy city sounds have not yet tired.

Walking all the way, everything on the street slipped past me unintentionally. Suddenly, I remembered the scene of [Roar, China] in Tokyo four years ago on a certain night.

I remember it was an early winter evening, the air in Tokyo was already very cold. I was invited by two friends to run to the new Tsukiji Theater in the middle of the night to watch the preview of [Roar, China].

When the time came, the workers were working with enthusiasm and courage; the audience were also excitedly staring and watching attentively. The atmosphere in the theater gradually became tense, and sympathetic anger filled everyone's hearts - the actors' hearts, the audience's hearts, roaring, the people in the theater, suddenly the entire theater was filled with roars, almost breaking the four walls of the theater.

We watched for half the night, until the next morning, and walked out of the theater extremely excitedly, returning to our own residence, the rose-colored sun had already climbed onto the eastern horizon. I really wanted to see their public performance again, but the evening was my return date, there was no way, so I left Tokyo at night.

Thinking, thinking, the theater arrived, I entered with a ticket, the huge venue was already full of people watching the play, I looked around, and found that almost every row of seats had friends sitting there, even those who were not my friends seemed quite familiar.

The curtain opened, a group of people in the colony - China struggling in suffering, being scolded and beaten by the so-called white foreign merchants, the incident gradually unfolded, these coolies had contact with the compliant people of a certain empire, because the coolies of the colony China had beaten to death foreign merchants who had white skin like them, so on the stage there burned the flames of repayment, producing various postures such as abuse, oppression, strangulation, and struggle. Now what we are seeing are these, these sufferings often suffered by colonial countries, what is planted in our hearts are the seeds of repayment, resistance, and struggle. Similarly, the comrades of the drama troupe are working tensely on the stage, the audience are watching enthusiastically and attentively, the atmosphere of the drama is getting thicker, the hearts of the audience are becoming tense, and finally, similarly, there appeared the roaring sounds of repayment. We, the people in the entire theater, as long as we were people, all roared, and immediately, the roar filled the entire theater, and the four walls almost burst.

At this time, the people in the Golden Grand Theater were roaring, and perhaps all parts of China were roaring like this. The imperialists are only invading day by day, and the people of the semi-colonial countries have long been involved in the anti-imperialist wave and are only shouting, Roar! China! Roar! Yes, China will eventually roar.

Brilliant and passionate light shone on the stage, and the tragic play ended here. The order of the audience became chaotic, and they swarmed out towards the entrance, Repayment, resistance, struggle, filling everyone's enthusiastic hearts - your heart, my heart, his heart, the hearts of all colonial slaves!

I walked to my residence very excitedly, the hot blood in my heart was boiling, the roars of the crowd had not yet disappeared from my ears, I thought... China is destined to roar, roar, China! Roar, China!

The Closed Door (3)

— Written by Henri de Regnier, Translated by Li Wanju

Below is what the voice said:

[Ah! Those poor worms, they don't even know what they're doing. Among this group of people, not one of them considers the fate of the motherland! They sacrifice everything for their current, insignificant benefits. Don't they even know that the future will use that merciless scale to weigh their actions! Is there not one among them who is willing to denounce their actions to themselves and make them consider their decency? Ah! If I were there, I would point out to them the abyss of shame they are rushing towards, and they would adopt my words, because everyone used to listen to me. But, now, it's over. I strangled myself with my own hands. The door to my life is closed forever. And now, who will still think of me, think of Lanweier, think of Maurice Lanweier! Ah! How miserable! How miserable! ......]

A rough punch, hitting a piece of furniture, which immediately crashed down, and at the same time I heard a woman's sobbing, choked with sobs.

Maurice Lanweier! Suddenly, I understood. Maurice Lanweier! This scandal twenty years apart floated into my mind again. I remembered the name I heard people talking about when I was a child, related to a famous scandal. Lanweier, this was the politician whose brilliant future suddenly sank into an irreparable failure. Lanweier, he was an eloquent and authoritative speaker, he was the leader of an important faction in the parliament, he had his glorious era, that fleeting glorious era. And I also remembered the seriousness of the situation at that time, the fierce threats from foreigners, the chaos in the country, and the enthusiastic words of Lanweier that inspired a brilliant patriotic movement, re-debating a memorable meeting of the congress. Later, on the day after the victory, when everyone's hopes were pinned on the one who seemed to be regarded as [the master of the era], Lanweier suddenly disappeared. I remembered his strange disappearance, his secret escape. Lanweier abandoned everything... family, responsibility, motherland... and eloped with a young woman he loved but could not marry. For her, he sacrificed his reputation and glory with love.

What I heard behind the door was Maurice Lanweier, who had changed his name to Mr. Duerlan Zhi, reminiscing about his past life, his authority as a speaker, and regretting the meaningless sacrifice he made in a moment of passion in the past. So I couldn't help but sadly think about the woman who was now silent in two layers of silence, the sobbing choke she just made. How much pain and what kind of guilt did she pay to exchange for that momentary intoxication of being loved? Ah! Poor people, when they conceal that famous love affair under a pseudonym, living such a wandering and exiled life, what has their love left them? What a fate, when the daily newspapers are delivered, sitting around a tea table in an ordinary hotel, in this remote place in the countryside, they formed a pair of [thought-provoking couples], and people who passed by here left with their sad image.

If the two Englishmen in the large living room hadn't woken me up when they went back to their rooms, it was already time for me to go back to sleep, I would have been meditating in front of their closed door for a long time. Because I have to leave early in the morning the next day, I should go to bed early. (The End)

Vacuum Tube Usage Guide

— Ming Xiang

Vacuum tubes, known as the soul of wireless radios, occupy the most important position in all wireless radios and are also of high value, so extreme caution must be taken when using them. If they are not used properly, it will lightly shorten their lifespan and affect the efficiency of the entire machine, and seriously destroy them in an instant. Here are a few notes on usage as a motto for wireless radio enthusiasts.

1. The copper pins of the vacuum tube must be kept very clean, and so must the spring pieces of the lamp holder. The contact point between the copper pin and the lamp holder must be tightly sealed, otherwise, it is very easy to cause problems. 2. The filament voltage must not exceed the specified value. If it does not have much impact on the radio reception effect, it is best to use only three-quarters of the specified value. This point can extend the lifespan of the vacuum tube.

2. The voltage of the C battery that supplies the grid negative potential (in AC machines, the voltage drop on the resistor is often used) must be accurate, otherwise, it is very easy to cause distortion.

3. The plate voltage should not be too low, otherwise, it will reduce the volume. If the power source is obtained from the voltage divider of the rectifier section, it must be measured with a voltmeter with extremely high resistance, approximately 1000 ohms per volt, to be accurate.

4. The work that the vacuum tube undertakes in the wireless radio must also be in accordance with what the manufacturer has stipulated. Inappropriate work is difficult to handle.

5. Vacuum tubes with extremely high amplification factor (HiginMu) cannot be used in transformer-coupled amplification circuits, as this combination will inevitably distort the sound quality.

6. For dry battery vacuum tubes (commonly known as power-saving light bulbs, such as 199, 109, 074, etc.), the filament voltage must absolutely not exceed the specified value, as their filaments are most easily burned out. 8. For AC vacuum tubes, the plate grid circuit is best connected to the center tap of the secondary coil of the power transformer that supplies the filament voltage, or a center-divided resistor can also be used. This connection can reduce the interference of AC noise.

7. Vacuum tubes cannot be subjected to severe vibrations. They must be stable when the filament is heated and used, so lamp holders with meticulous designs often have springs installed to avoid damage to the filament of the vacuum tube due to vibration.

8. A small number of thorium-coated filament vacuum tubes, such as 201A199222, etc., may occasionally fail to emit electrons after being used improperly or for too long (commonly known as silent light bulbs). They can still be revived with appropriate methods. The revival method will be described in another article.

The Natural Wavelength of a Single-Wire Antenna

— Yi Zhi

It is often heard that my antenna is 75 feet long, and it receives the sound from Station A very well, but if I change it to 100 feet, the sound from Station B is louder than that from Station A. What is the reason for this? It turns out that the antenna itself, like a choke coil, has inductance, capacitance, and resistance, so it has its own natural wavelength. If the wavelength of the station you are receiving matches the wavelength of your antenna, then the resonance is the most sensitive, and the induced power is the strongest. The input signal voltage of your radio receiver is large, and the volume will naturally be louder.

The inductance, capacitance, and resistance of the antenna can be represented by the diagram: A is the antenna, C is the ground wire, L shows its inductance, R shows its resistance, and C shows its capacitance.

The formula for the inductance of a single-wire horizontal antenna is:

L=2L（23logto2h1+14）X10-3·····（mh）

The formula for the capacitance of a single-wire horizontal antenna is:

C=L-46log102hrx1-9·····（mmf）

L is the inductance, the unit is megahenry (uh). C is the capacitance, the unit is microfarad (uuf). Ｉ is the length of the antenna, r is the radius of the wire, and h is the distance between the wire and the ground.

From the above two formulas, it can be seen that the natural wavelength of the antenna is absolutely related to the length, height, and wire diameter of the antenna. If the antenna is lengthened, the inductance, capacitance, and resistance will all increase. If the antenna is raised, it will only increase its inductance and decrease its capacitance, while the resistance will remain unchanged. If the length of the antenna is shortened or its height is lowered, the opposite is true. A sensitive antenna must have a large inductance and a small capacitance and resistance, so the higher the antenna is, the better.

Calculating the natural wavelength of a single-wire antenna is a bit troublesome, so I will omit it here. Now I will introduce a wavelength table that has already been calculated, and excerpt it below for reference:

Antenna Natural Wavelength Table

100 143 151 162 185

75 113 121 128 157

60 95 104 113 136

30 59 69 80 102

Horizontal Length (feet) Natural Wavelength (meters) Height (feet) 20 30 40 60

Ground Wire Testing Method

— Li Yuanqing

Many people who install radios think that as long as the antenna is installed meticulously, they can get excellent results. Therefore, they think that the ground wire is unimportant. In fact, the mission of the ground wire in the radio is no less important than the antenna.

A bad ground wire will not only have a significant impact on the radio reception results, but also easily cause various noises - especially in AC machines, it is more likely to increase AC hum or generate many strange noises.

Whether the ground wire is good or not depends on the amount of its own resistance. There are of course many ways to test the ground wire resistance, but if there is no sophisticated instrument, it is impossible to start for a while.

Ordinary external power lines (electric light lines or power lines, etc.) probably have one wire connected to the ground wire. (See the left side of the attached diagram) If you use this point to install, you can solve the above difficulties.

First measure the external voltage with a voltmeter as usual (see the dotted line in the figure). If the measured value is Ei, then change one end of the voltmeter to receive the radio ground wire, and the other end is still connected to the power line A (it is impossible to know which of the AB lines is the ground wire, so you can switch them). At this time, the value (E2) shown by the voltmeter pointer, if...

(1) Drops to zero, it proves that the ground wire is broken.

(2) Trembles incessantly, it proves that the ground wire contact point is bad, or it is about to break.

(3) Differs greatly from E1, it proves that the ground wire itself has a large resistance.

(4) Is slightly smaller than E1, it proves that the ground wire itself has a slight resistance.

(5) Is close to or equal to E1, it proves that the ground wire itself has extremely low resistance.

Commemorating Edison

— Ke Ming

Tomorrow, October 8th, is the second anniversary of Edison's death. This day is one that everyone should remember. Edison's life deeds and his personality are so worthy of respect and emulation by our young people. It is not known how many things he invented. He once tried [space telegraph] to create the term [etheric power]. He also discovered that electrons are emitted from the hot filament when experimenting with electric lights, which is the so-called [Edison effect]. This was very helpful for the later invention of vacuum tubes.

Before the age of fifty-five, Edison averaged nineteen and a half hours of work per day. When inventing the phonograph, he even worked for five days and nights at a time. In his youth, he liked to try all the experiments in books one by one. He did not pay attention to clothes and decorations, but he was not stingy at all when it came to buying books, instruments, and medicines.

Because of commemorating Edison, we feel how much our country needs inventors. Our country is already in a serious situation of internal and external troubles, so we hope that there can also be an Edison born in China to save the people from suffering with great inventions and place the country in a state of stability.

Finally, we quote one of Edison's famous sayings: [Genius is one percent inspiration and ninety-nine percent perspiration.]

Repairing and Reconstructing Electrical Capacitors

— ]Zhibing

In all radio AC generators, within their power supply circuits, there exists something called a filter. Its composition is a combination of a choke coil and a fixed capacitor. These capacitors have a large capacity and must be capable of handling high voltage loads. Therefore, their construction is difficult and their value is high. Because they are located in high-voltage circuits, they are very prone to damage. Therefore, people who study radio often discard them because they are difficult to repair, which is a pity and a helpless situation.

Now, there is a method for repairing and reconstructing them, written below. Fellow radio enthusiasts, please follow this method and try it out, and you may be able to recover a small portion of your lost money.

To know how to repair them, you must first understand their construction. The construction of these capacitors is very simple: two long strips of tin foil are rolled up with three long strips of waxed paper in between (some are parallel combinations of two, three, or four sets of rolled-up capacitors). The purpose of the three strips of waxed paper is to insulate the two strips of tin foil. The cause of their damage is that a small portion of the insulation is poor or broken, causing the two tin foils to short-circuit, thus losing their capacitance function.

To repair them, carefully disassemble the outer metal or cardboard casing, and carefully scrape off any wax or sealing wax adhering to its surroundings. Then, unfold the capacitor, which consists of three layers of waxed paper and two layers of tin foil rolled up. Cut off a square from the remaining part of the tin foil extending from the outer end of the waxed paper. Patch the damaged area of the waxed paper layer by layer, roll it up again as before, and reinstall it in its original place and try it. The function should remain unchanged. The following are some points to note when unfolding for repair and re-rolling:

(1) Points to note when unfolding:

1. After the outer casing is disassembled, the wax adhering to the capacitor must be carefully scraped off without damaging the waxed paper and tin foil of the capacitor.

2. Do not use fire to melt the wax, as this may burn the waxed paper and melt the tin foil.

3. When unfolding the capacitor, be careful not to tear the waxed paper or pull and break the edges, as it will be difficult to roll it back to its original shape.

4. When unfolding to the burnt area of the capacitor, check how many layers are burnt and remove all the burnt layers. However, do not unfold all the way, only to the last layer. (To be continued)
